aaa attribute format BNG-DOMAIN
 username-strip prefix-delimiter @
!
aaa attribute format NAS-PORT-ID
 circuit-id plus remote-id
!
aaa radius attribute nas-port format e PPPPPPQQQQQQQQQQVVVVVVVVVVUUUUUU type 37
aaa radius attribute nas-port-id format NAS-PORT-ID
aaa accounting subscriber PPP_USER_AUTHEN_AUTHOR group BNG_RADIUS
aaa authorization subscriber PPP_USER_AUTHEN_AUTHOR group BNG_RADIUS
aaa authentication subscriber PPP_USER_AUTHEN_AUTHOR group BNG_RADIUS
pppoe bba-group BNG_PPPOE
 service selection disable
 sessions mac throttle 10 20 30
 sessions outer-vlan limit 4000
 invalid-session-id log
!
pppoe in-flight-window 200
class-map type control subscriber match-all PPP-SUBS
 match protocol ppp 
 end-class-map
! 
!
class-map type control subscriber match-all PPP-SUBS-celcombiz
 match protocol ppp 
 match domain celcombiz format BNG-DOMAIN
 end-class-map
! 
class-map type control subscriber match-all PPP-SUBS-celcomhome
 match protocol ppp 
 match domain celcomhome format BNG-DOMAIN
 end-class-map
! 
class-map type control subscriber match-all PPP-SUBS-fixed.celcombizctsb
 match protocol ppp 
 match domain fixed.celcombizctsb format BNG-DOMAIN
 end-class-map
! 
class-map type control subscriber match-all PPP-SUBS-celcomfirstfibre.com.my
 match protocol ppp 
 match domain celcomfirstfibre.com.my format BNG-DOMAIN
 end-class-map
! 
policy-map type control subscriber OLT-BE1000-HSI
 event session-start match-first
  class type control subscriber PPP-SUBS do-until-failure
   10 activate dynamic-template PPP-START
  ! 
 ! 
 event session-activate match-first
  class type control subscriber PPP-SUBS-celcomhome do-until-failure
   10 authenticate aaa list PPP_USER_AUTHEN_AUTHOR
   20 activate dynamic-template PPP-ACTIVATE-HSI-celcomhome
  ! 
  class type control subscriber PPP-SUBS-celcomfirstfibre.com.my do-until-failure
   10 authenticate aaa list PPP_USER_AUTHEN_AUTHOR
   20 activate dynamic-template PPP-ACTIVATE-HSI-celcomfirstfibre.com.my
  ! 
 ! 
 end-policy-map
! 
policy-map type control subscriber OLT-BE1000-HSI_SME
 event session-start match-first
  class type control subscriber PPP-SUBS do-until-failure
   10 activate dynamic-template PPP-START
  ! 
 ! 
 event session-activate match-first
  class type control subscriber PPP-SUBS-celcombiz do-until-failure
   10 authenticate aaa list PPP_USER_AUTHEN_AUTHOR
   20 activate dynamic-template PPP-ACTIVATE-HSI_SME-celcombiz
  ! 
  class type control subscriber PPP-SUBS-fixed.celcombizctsb do-until-failure
   10 authenticate aaa list PPP_USER_AUTHEN_AUTHOR
   20 activate dynamic-template PPP-ACTIVATE-HSI_SME-fixed.celcombizctsb
  ! 
 ! 
 end-policy-map
! 
ssh client dscp 16
ssh server dscp 16
ssh server rate-limit 600
ssh server session-limit 10
ssh server v2
ssh server vrf default ipv4 access-list VTY-ACL
track BNG-BE1000
 type line-protocol state
  interface Bundle-Ether1000
 !
!
track BNG-BE1001
 type line-protocol state
  interface Bundle-Ether1001
 !
!
track GE_0-3-0-37
 type line-protocol state
  interface GigabitEthernet0/3/0/37
 !
!
track GE_0-3-0-39
 type line-protocol state
  interface GigabitEthernet0/3/0/39
 !
!
ipsla
 responder
  twamp
   timeout 600
  !
 !
 server twamp
  timer inactivity 600
 !
!
telnet vrf default ipv4 server max-servers 100
end
